            - generic [ref=e213]:
              - heading "Page" [level=1] [ref=e215]
              - paragraph [ref=e216]:
                - text: Page provides methods to interact with a single tab in a
                - link "Browser" [ref=e217] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-browser
                - text: ", or an"
                - link "extension background page" [ref=e218] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://developer.chrome.com/extensions/background_pages
                - text: in Chromium. One
                - link "Browser" [ref=e219] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-browser
                - text: instance might have multiple
                - link "Page" [ref=e220] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page
                - text: instances.
              - paragraph [ref=e221]: "This example creates a page, navigates it to a URL, and then saves a screenshot:"
              - code [ref=e225]:
                - generic [ref=e226]: "const { webkit } = require('playwright'); // Or 'chromium' or 'firefox'."
                - generic [ref=e227]: "(async () => {"
                - generic [ref=e228]: const browser = await webkit.launch();
                - generic [ref=e229]: const context = await browser.newContext();
                - generic [ref=e230]: const page = await context.newPage();
                - generic [ref=e231]: await page.goto('https://example.com');
                - generic [ref=e232]: "await page.screenshot({ path: 'screenshot.png' });"
                - generic [ref=e233]: await browser.close();
                - generic [ref=e234]: "})();"
              - paragraph [ref=e235]:
                - text: The Page class emits various events (described below) which can be handled using any of Node's native
                - link "EventEmitter" [ref=e236] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://nodejs.org/api/events.html#events_class_eventemitter
                  - code [ref=e237]: EventEmitter
                - text: methods, such as
                - code [ref=e238]: "on"
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e239]: once
                - text: or
                - code [ref=e240]: removeListener
                - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e241]:
                - text: This example logs a message for a single page
                - code [ref=e242]: load
                - text: "event:"
              - code [ref=e246]:
                - generic [ref=e247]: page.once('load', () => console.log('Page loaded!'));
              - paragraph [ref=e248]:
                - text: To unsubscribe from events use the
                - code [ref=e249]: removeListener
                - text: "method:"
              - code [ref=e253]:
                - generic [ref=e254]: "function logRequest(interceptedRequest) {"
                - generic [ref=e255]: console.log('A request was made:', interceptedRequest.url());
                - generic [ref=e256]: "}"
                - generic [ref=e257]: page.on('request', logRequest);
                - generic [ref=e258]: // Sometime later...
                - generic [ref=e259]: page.removeListener('request', logRequest);
              - separator [ref=e260]
              - heading "MethodsDirect link to Methods" [level=2] [ref=e261]:
                - text: Methods

              - heading "addInitScriptDirect link to addInitScript" [level=3] [ref=e263]:
                - text: addInitScript
                - link "Direct link to addInitScript" [ref=e264] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#page-add-init-script"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: Added before v1.9
              - paragraph [ref=e265]: "Adds a script which would be evaluated in one of the following scenarios:"
              - list [ref=e266]:
                - listitem [ref=e267]: Whenever the page is navigated.
                - listitem [ref=e268]: Whenever the child frame is attached or navigated. In this case, the script is evaluated in the context of the newly attached frame.
              - paragraph [ref=e269]:
                - text: The script is evaluated after the document was created but before any of its scripts were run. This is useful to amend the JavaScript environment, e.g. to seed
                - code [ref=e270]: Math.random
                - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e271]:
                - strong [ref=e272]: Usage
              - paragraph [ref=e273]:
                - text: An example of overriding
                - code [ref=e274]: Math.random
                - text: "before the page loads:"
              - code [ref=e278]:
                - generic [ref=e279]: // preload.js
                - generic [ref=e280]: Math.random = () => 42;
              - code [ref=e284]:
                - generic [ref=e285]: // In your playwright script, assuming the preload.js file is in same directory
                - generic [ref=e286]: "await page.addInitScript({ path: './preload.js' });"
              - code [ref=e290]:
                - generic [ref=e291]: "await page.addInitScript(mock => {"
                - generic [ref=e292]: window.mock = mock;
                - generic [ref=e293]: "}, mock);"
              - generic [ref=e294]:
                - generic [ref=e295]:
                  - img [ref=e297]
                  - text: note
                - paragraph [ref=e300]:
                  - text: The order of evaluation of multiple scripts installed via
                  - link "browserContext.addInitScript()" [ref=e301] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-add-init-script
                  - text: and
                  - link "page.addInitScript()" [ref=e302] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-add-init-script
                  - text: is not defined.
              - paragraph [ref=e303]:
                - strong [ref=e304]: Arguments
              - list [ref=e305]:
                - listitem [ref=e306]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e307]:
                    - code [ref=e308]: script
                    - link "function" [ref=e309] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Function
                    - text: "|"
                    - link "string" [ref=e310] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                    - text: "|"
                    - link "Object" [ref=e311] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object
                    - link "#" [ref=e312] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: "#page-add-init-script-option-script"
                  - list [ref=e313]:
                    - listitem [ref=e314]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e315]:
                        - code [ref=e316]: path
                        - link "string" [ref=e317] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                        - emphasis [ref=e318]: (optional)
                      - paragraph [ref=e319]:
                        - text: Path to the JavaScript file. If
                        - code [ref=e320]: path
                        - text: is a relative path, then it is resolved relative to the current working directory. Optional.
                    - listitem [ref=e321]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e322]:
                        - code [ref=e323]: content
                        - link "string" [ref=e324] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                        - emphasis [ref=e325]: (optional)
                      - paragraph [ref=e326]: Raw script content. Optional.
                  - paragraph [ref=e327]: Script to be evaluated in the page.
                - listitem [ref=e328]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e329]:
                    - code [ref=e330]: arg
                    - link "Serializable" [ref=e331] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/JSON/stringify#Description
                    - emphasis [ref=e332]: (optional)
                    - link "#" [ref=e333] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: "#page-add-init-script-option-arg"
                  - paragraph [ref=e334]:
                    - text: Optional argument to pass to
                    - link "script" [ref=e335] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-add-init-script-option-script
                    - text: (only supported when passing a function).
              - paragraph [ref=e336]:
                - strong [ref=e337]: Returns
              - list [ref=e338]:
                - listitem [ref=e339]:
                  - link "Promise" [ref=e340] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Promise
                  - text: <
                  - link "void" [ref=e341] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/undefined
                  - text: ">"
                  - link "#" [ref=e342] [cursor=pointer]:

              - separator [ref=e343]
              - heading "addLocatorHandlerDirect link to addLocatorHandler" [level=3] [ref=e344]:
                - text: addLocatorHandler
                - link "Direct link to addLocatorHandler" [ref=e345] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#page-add-locator-handler"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: "Added in: v1.42"
              - paragraph [ref=e346]: When testing a web page, sometimes unexpected overlays like a "Sign up" dialog appear and block actions you want to automate, e.g. clicking a button. These overlays don't always show up in the same way or at the same time, making them tricky to handle in automated tests.
              - paragraph [ref=e347]: This method lets you set up a special function, called a handler, that activates when it detects that overlay is visible. The handler's job is to remove the overlay, allowing your test to continue as if the overlay wasn't there.
              - paragraph [ref=e348]: "Things to keep in mind:"
              - list [ref=e349]:
                - listitem [ref=e350]:
                  - text: When an overlay is shown predictably, we recommend explicitly waiting for it in your test and dismissing it as a part of your normal test flow, instead of using
                  - link "page.addLocatorHandler()" [ref=e351] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-add-locator-handler
                  - text: .
                - listitem [ref=e352]:
                  - text: Playwright checks for the overlay every time before executing or retrying an action that requires an
                  - link "actionability check" [ref=e353] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/actionability
                  - text: ", or before performing an auto-waiting assertion check. When overlay is visible, Playwright calls the handler first, and then proceeds with the action/assertion. Note that the handler is only called when you perform an action/assertion - if the overlay becomes visible but you don't perform any actions, the handler will not be triggered."
                - listitem [ref=e354]:
                  - text: After executing the handler, Playwright will ensure that overlay that triggered the handler is not visible anymore. You can opt-out of this behavior with
                  - link "noWaitAfter" [ref=e355] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-add-locator-handler-option-no-wait-after
                  - text: .
                - listitem [ref=e356]: The execution time of the handler counts towards the timeout of the action/assertion that executed the handler. If your handler takes too long, it might cause timeouts.
                - listitem [ref=e357]: You can register multiple handlers. However, only a single handler will be running at a time. Make sure the actions within a handler don't depend on another handler.
              - generic [ref=e358]:
                - generic [ref=e359]:
                  - img [ref=e361]
                  - text: warning
                - generic [ref=e363]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e364]: Running the handler will alter your page state mid-test. For example it will change the currently focused element and move the mouse. Make sure that actions that run after the handler are self-contained and do not rely on the focus and mouse state being unchanged.
                  - paragraph [ref=e365]:
                    - text: For example, consider a test that calls
                    - link "locator.focus()" [ref=e366] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-focus
                    - text: followed by
                    - link "keyboard.press()" [ref=e367] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: /docs/api/class-keyboard#keyboard-press
                    - text: . If your handler clicks a button between these two actions, the focused element most likely will be wrong, and key press will happen on the unexpected element. Use
                    - link "locator.press()" [ref=e368] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-press
                    - text: instead to avoid this problem.
                  - paragraph [ref=e369]:
                    - text: Another example is a series of mouse actions, where
                    - link "mouse.move()" [ref=e370] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: /docs/api/class-mouse#mouse-move
                    - text: is followed by
                    - link "mouse.down()" [ref=e371] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: /docs/api/class-mouse#mouse-down
                    - text: . Again, when the handler runs between these two actions, the mouse position will be wrong during the mouse down. Prefer self-contained actions like
                    - link "locator.click()" [ref=e372] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-click
                    - text: that do not rely on the state being unchanged by a handler.

              - paragraph [ref=e1674]:
                - strong [ref=e1675]: Details
              - paragraph [ref=e1676]:
                - text: Role selector
                - strong [ref=e1677]: does not replace
                - text: accessibility audits and conformance tests, but rather gives early feedback about the ARIA guidelines.
              - paragraph [ref=e1678]:
                - text: Many html elements have an implicitly
                - link "defined role" [ref=e1679] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://w3c.github.io/html-aam/#html-element-role-mappings
                - text: that is recognized by the role selector. You can find all the
                - link "supported roles here" [ref=e1680] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://www.w3.org/TR/wai-aria-1.2/#role_definitions
                - text: . ARIA guidelines
                - strong [ref=e1681]: do not recommend
                - text: duplicating implicit roles and attributes by setting
                - code [ref=e1682]: role
                - text: and/or
                - code [ref=e1683]: aria-*
                - text: attributes to default values.
              - separator [ref=e1684]

              - paragraph [ref=e1687]: Locate element by the test id.
              - paragraph [ref=e1688]:
                - strong [ref=e1689]: Usage
              - paragraph [ref=e1690]: Consider the following DOM structure.
              - code [ref=e1694]:
                - generic [ref=e1695]: <button data-testid="directions">Itinraire</button>

              - code [ref=e1700]:

                - strong [ref=e1703]: Arguments
              - list [ref=e1704]:

                  - paragraph [ref=e1706]:
                    - code [ref=e1707]: testId
                    - link "string" [ref=e1708] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                    - text: "|"

              - paragraph [ref=e1712]:
                - strong [ref=e1713]: Returns
              - list [ref=e1714]:

                  - link "Locator" [ref=e1716] [cursor=pointer]:

                    - /url: "#page-get-by-test-id-return"
              - paragraph [ref=e1718]:
                - strong [ref=e1719]: Details
              - paragraph [ref=e1720]:
                - text: By default, the
                - code [ref=e1721]: data-testid
                - text: attribute is used as a test id. Use
                - link "selectors.setTestIdAttribute()" [ref=e1722] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-selectors#selectors-set-test-id-attribute
                - text: to configure a different test id attribute if necessary.
              - code [ref=e1726]:
                - generic [ref=e1727]: "// Set custom test id attribute from @playwright/test config:"
                - generic [ref=e1728]: "import { defineConfig } from '@playwright/test';"
                - generic [ref=e1729]: "export default defineConfig({"
                - generic [ref=e1730]: "use: {"
                - generic [ref=e1731]: "testIdAttribute: 'data-pw'"
                - generic [ref=e1732]: "},"
                - generic [ref=e1733]: "});"
              - separator [ref=e1734]
              - heading "getByTextDirect link to getByText" [level=3] [ref=e1735]:
                - text: getByText
                - link "Direct link to getByText" [ref=e1736] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#page-get-by-text"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: "Added in: v1.27"
              - paragraph [ref=e1737]: Allows locating elements that contain given text.
              - paragraph [ref=e1738]:
                - text: See also
                - link "locator.filter()" [ref=e1739] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-locator#locator-filter
                - text: that allows to match by another criteria, like an accessible role, and then filter by the text content.
              - paragraph [ref=e1740]:
                - strong [ref=e1741]: Usage
              - paragraph [ref=e1742]: "Consider the following DOM structure:"
              - code [ref=e1746]:
                - generic [ref=e1747]: <div>Hello <span>world</span></div>
                - generic [ref=e1748]: <div>Hello</div>
              - paragraph [ref=e1749]: "You can locate by text substring, exact string, or a regular expression:"
              - code [ref=e1753]:
                - generic [ref=e1754]: // Matches <span>
                - generic [ref=e1755]: page.getByText('world');
                - generic [ref=e1756]: // Matches first <div>
                - generic [ref=e1757]: page.getByText('Hello world');
                - generic [ref=e1758]: // Matches second <div>
                - generic [ref=e1759]: "page.getByText('Hello', { exact: true });"
                - generic [ref=e1760]: // Matches both <div>s
                - generic [ref=e1761]: page.getByText(/Hello/);
                - generic [ref=e1762]: // Matches second <div>
                - generic [ref=e1763]: page.getByText(/^hello$/i);

              - paragraph [ref=e1793]:
                - strong [ref=e1794]: Details
              - paragraph [ref=e1795]: Matching by text always normalizes whitespace, even with exact match. For example, it turns multiple spaces into one, turns line breaks into spaces and ignores leading and trailing whitespace.
              - paragraph [ref=e1796]:
                - text: Input elements of the type
                - code [ref=e1797]: button
                - text: and
                - code [ref=e1798]: submit
                - text: are matched by their
                - code [ref=e1799]: value
                - text: instead of the text content. For example, locating by text
                - code [ref=e1800]: "\"Log in\""
                - text: matches
                - code [ref=e1801]: <input type=button value="Log in">
                - text: .

              - paragraph [ref=e1978]: Returns the main resource response. In case of multiple redirects, the navigation will resolve with the first non-redirect response.
              - paragraph [ref=e1979]: "The method will throw an error if:"
              - list [ref=e1980]:
                - listitem [ref=e1981]: there's an SSL error (e.g. in case of self-signed certificates).
                - listitem [ref=e1982]: target URL is invalid.
                - listitem [ref=e1983]:
                  - text: the
                  - link "timeout" [ref=e1984] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-goto-option-timeout
                  - text: is exceeded during navigation.
                - listitem [ref=e1985]: the remote server does not respond or is unreachable.
                - listitem [ref=e1986]: the main resource failed to load.
              - paragraph [ref=e1987]:
                - text: The method will not throw an error when any valid HTTP status code is returned by the remote server, including 404 "Not Found" and 500 "Internal Server Error". The status code for such responses can be retrieved by calling
                - link "response.status()" [ref=e1988] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-response#response-status

                  - code [ref=e1996]: about:blank

                - text: locator
                - link "Direct link to locator" [ref=e2101] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#page-locator"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: "Added in: v1.14"
              - paragraph [ref=e2102]: The method returns an element locator that can be used to perform actions on this page / frame. Locator is resolved to the element immediately before performing an action, so a series of actions on the same locator can in fact be performed on different DOM elements. That would happen if the DOM structure between those actions has changed.
              - paragraph [ref=e2103]:
                - link "Learn more about locators" [ref=e2104] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/locators
                - text: .

                - strong [ref=e2114]: Arguments
              - list [ref=e2115]:
                - listitem [ref=e2116]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e2117]:
                    - code [ref=e2118]: selector

                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                    - link "#" [ref=e2120] [cursor=pointer]:

                  - paragraph [ref=e2121]: A selector to use when resolving DOM element.
                - listitem [ref=e2122]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e2123]:
                    - code [ref=e2124]: options
                    - link "Object" [ref=e2125] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object
                    - emphasis [ref=e2126]: (optional)
                  - list [ref=e2127]:
                    - listitem [ref=e2128]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2129]:
                        - code [ref=e2130]: has
                        - link "Locator" [ref=e2131] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-locator
                        - emphasis [ref=e2132]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e2133] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-locator-option-has"
                      - paragraph [ref=e2134]:
                        - text: Narrows down the results of the method to those which contain elements matching this relative locator. For example,
                        - code [ref=e2135]: article
                        - text: that has
                        - code [ref=e2136]: text=Playwright
                        - text: matches
                        - code [ref=e2137]: <article><div>Playwright</div></article>
                        - text: .
                      - paragraph [ref=e2138]:
                        - text: Inner locator
                        - strong [ref=e2139]: must be relative
                        - text: to the outer locator and is queried starting with the outer locator match, not the document root. For example, you can find
                        - code [ref=e2140]: content
                        - text: that has
                        - code [ref=e2141]: div
                        - text: in
                        - code [ref=e2142]: <article><content><div>Playwright</div></content></article>
                        - text: . However, looking for
                        - code [ref=e2143]: content
                        - text: that has
                        - code [ref=e2144]: article div
                        - text: will fail, because the inner locator must be relative and should not use any elements outside the
                        - code [ref=e2145]: content
                        - text: .
                      - paragraph [ref=e2146]:
                        - text: Note that outer and inner locators must belong to the same frame. Inner locator must not contain
                        - link "FrameLocator" [ref=e2147] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-framelocator
                        - text: s.
                    - listitem [ref=e2148]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2149]:
                        - code [ref=e2150]: hasNot
                        - link "Locator" [ref=e2151] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-locator
                        - emphasis [ref=e2152]: (optional)
                        - text: "Added in: v1.33"
                        - link "#" [ref=e2153] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-locator-option-has-not"
                      - paragraph [ref=e2154]:
                        - text: Matches elements that do not contain an element that matches an inner locator. Inner locator is queried against the outer one. For example,
                        - code [ref=e2155]: article
                        - text: that does not have
                        - code [ref=e2156]: div
                        - text: matches
                        - code [ref=e2157]: <article><span>Playwright</span></article>
                        - text: .
                      - paragraph [ref=e2158]:
                        - text: Note that outer and inner locators must belong to the same frame. Inner locator must not contain
                        - link "FrameLocator" [ref=e2159] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-framelocator
                        - text: s.
                    - listitem [ref=e2160]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2161]:
                        - code [ref=e2162]: hasNotText
                        - link "string" [ref=e2163] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                        - text: "|"
                        - link "RegExp" [ref=e2164] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/RegExp

                        - link "#" [ref=e2166] [cursor=pointer]:

                      - paragraph [ref=e2167]:
                        - text: Matches elements that do not contain specified text somewhere inside, possibly in a child or a descendant element. When passed a
                        - link "string" [ref=e2168] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                        - text: ", matching is case-insensitive and searches for a substring."
                    - listitem [ref=e2169]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2170]:
                        - code [ref=e2171]: hasText
                        - link "string" [ref=e2172] [cursor=pointer]:

                        - text: "|"

                        - link "#" [ref=e2175] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-locator-option-has-text"
                      - paragraph [ref=e2176]:
                        - text: Matches elements containing specified text somewhere inside, possibly in a child or a descendant element. When passed a
                        - link "string" [ref=e2177] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                        - text: ", matching is case-insensitive and searches for a substring. For example,"
                        - code [ref=e2178]: "\"Playwright\""
                        - text: matches
                        - code [ref=e2179]: <article><div>Playwright</div></article>

              - text: "Added in: v1.9"
              - paragraph [ref=e2247]:
                - text: Pauses script execution. Playwright will stop executing the script and wait for the user to either press the 'Resume' button in the page overlay or to call
                - code [ref=e2248]: playwright.resume()
                - text: in the DevTools console.
              - paragraph [ref=e2249]: User can inspect selectors or perform manual steps while paused. Resume will continue running the original script from the place it was paused.

              - paragraph [ref=e2275]: Returns the PDF buffer.
              - paragraph [ref=e2276]:
                - code [ref=e2277]: page.pdf()
                - text: generates a pdf of the page with
                - code [ref=e2278]: print
                - text: css media. To generate a pdf with
                - code [ref=e2279]: screen
                - text: media, call
                - link "page.emulateMedia()" [ref=e2280] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-emulate-media
                - text: before calling
                - code [ref=e2281]: page.pdf()
                - text: ":"
              - generic [ref=e2282]:
                - generic [ref=e2283]:
                  - img [ref=e2285]
                  - text: note
                - paragraph [ref=e2288]:
                  - text: By default,
                  - code [ref=e2289]: page.pdf()
                  - text: generates a pdf with modified colors for printing. Use the
                  - link "-webkit-print-color-adjust" [ref=e2290] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/-webkit-print-color-adjust
                    - code [ref=e2291]: "-webkit-print-color-adjust"
                  - text: property to force rendering of exact colors.
              - paragraph [ref=e2292]:

              - code [ref=e2297]:

                - generic [ref=e2300]: "await page.pdf({ path: 'page.pdf' });"

                - text: options accept values labeled with units. Unlabeled values are treated as pixels.

              - heading "reloadDirect link to reload" [level=3] [ref=e2539]:
                - text: reload
                - link "Direct link to reload" [ref=e2540] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#page-reload"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: Added before v1.9
              - paragraph [ref=e2541]: This method reloads the current page, in the same way as if the user had triggered a browser refresh. Returns the main resource response. In case of multiple redirects, the navigation will resolve with the response of the last redirect.
              - paragraph [ref=e2542]:
                - strong [ref=e2543]: Usage
              - code [ref=e2547]:
                - generic [ref=e2548]: await page.reload();
                - generic [ref=e2549]: await page.reload(options);
              - paragraph [ref=e2550]:
                - strong [ref=e2551]: Arguments
              - list [ref=e2552]:
                - listitem [ref=e2553]:
                  - code [ref=e2554]: options
                  - link "Object" [ref=e2555] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object
                  - emphasis [ref=e2556]: (optional)
                  - list [ref=e2557]:
                    - listitem [ref=e2558]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2559]:
                        - code [ref=e2560]: timeout
                        - link "number" [ref=e2561] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#Number_type
                        - emphasis [ref=e2562]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e2563] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-reload-option-timeout"
                      - paragraph [ref=e2564]:
                        - text: Maximum operation time in milliseconds. Defaults to
                        - code [ref=e2565]: "0"
                        - text: "- no timeout. The default value can be changed via"
                        - code [ref=e2566]: navigationTimeout
                        - text: option in the config, or by using the
                        - link "browserContext.setDefaultNavigationTimeout()" [ref=e2567] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-set-default-navigation-timeout
                        - text: ","
                        - link "browserContext.setDefaultTimeout()" [ref=e2568] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-set-default-timeout
                        - text: ","
                        - link "page.setDefaultNavigationTimeout()" [ref=e2569] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-set-default-navigation-timeout
                        - text: or
                        - link "page.setDefaultTimeout()" [ref=e2570] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-set-default-timeout
                        - text: methods.
                    - listitem [ref=e2571]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2572]:
                        - code [ref=e2573]: waitUntil
                        - text: "\"load\" | \"domcontentloaded\" | \"networkidle\" | \"commit\""
                        - emphasis [ref=e2574]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e2575] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-reload-option-wait-until"
                      - paragraph [ref=e2576]:
                        - text: When to consider operation succeeded, defaults to
                        - code [ref=e2577]: load
                        - text: ". Events can be either:"
                      - list [ref=e2578]:
                        - listitem [ref=e2579]:
                          - code [ref=e2580]: "'domcontentloaded'"
                          - text: "- consider operation to be finished when the"
                          - code [ref=e2581]: DOMContentLoaded
                          - text: event is fired.
                        - listitem [ref=e2582]:
                          - code [ref=e2583]: "'load'"
                          - text: "- consider operation to be finished when the"
                          - code [ref=e2584]: load
                          - text: event is fired.
                        - listitem [ref=e2585]:
                          - code [ref=e2586]: "'networkidle'"
                          - text: "-"
                          - strong [ref=e2587]: DISCOURAGED
                          - text: consider operation to be finished when there are no network connections for at least
                          - code [ref=e2588]: "500"
                          - text: ms. Don't use this method for testing, rely on web assertions to assess readiness instead.
                        - listitem [ref=e2589]:
                          - code [ref=e2590]: "'commit'"
                          - text: "- consider operation to be finished when network response is received and the document started loading."

              - heading "removeAllListenersDirect link to removeAllListeners" [level=3] [ref=e2600]:
                - text: removeAllListeners
                - link "Direct link to removeAllListeners" [ref=e2601] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#page-remove-all-listeners"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: "Added in: v1.47"
              - paragraph [ref=e2602]: Removes all the listeners of the given type (or all registered listeners if no type given). Allows to wait for async listeners to complete or to ignore subsequent errors from these listeners.
              - paragraph [ref=e2603]:
                - strong [ref=e2604]: Usage
              - code [ref=e2608]:
                - generic [ref=e2609]: "page.on('request', async request => {"
                - generic [ref=e2610]: const response = await request.response();
                - generic [ref=e2611]: const body = await response.body();
                - generic [ref=e2612]: console.log(body.byteLength);
                - generic [ref=e2613]: "});"
                - generic [ref=e2614]: "await page.goto('https://playwright.dev', { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });"
                - generic [ref=e2615]: // Waits for all the reported 'request' events to resolve.
                - generic [ref=e2616]: "await page.removeAllListeners('request', { behavior: 'wait' });"
              - paragraph [ref=e2617]:
                - strong [ref=e2618]: Arguments
              - list [ref=e2619]:
                - listitem [ref=e2620]:
                  - code [ref=e2621]: type
                  - link "string" [ref=e2622] [cursor=pointer]:

                  - emphasis [ref=e2628]: (optional)
                  - list [ref=e2629]:
                    - listitem [ref=e2630]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2631]:
                        - code [ref=e2632]: behavior
                        - text: "\"wait\" | \"ignoreErrors\" | \"default\""
                        - emphasis [ref=e2633]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e2634] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-remove-all-listeners-option-behavior"
                      - paragraph [ref=e2635]: "Specifies whether to wait for already running listeners and what to do if they throw errors:"
                      - list [ref=e2636]:
                        - listitem [ref=e2637]:
                          - code [ref=e2638]: "'default'"
                          - text: "- do not wait for current listener calls (if any) to finish, if the listener throws, it may result in unhandled error"
                        - listitem [ref=e2639]:
                          - code [ref=e2640]: "'wait'"
                          - text: "- wait for current listener calls (if any) to finish"
                        - listitem [ref=e2641]:
                          - code [ref=e2642]: "'ignoreErrors'"
                          - text: "- do not wait for current listener calls (if any) to finish, all errors thrown by the listeners after removal are silently caught"

              - heading "requestGCDirect link to requestGC" [level=3] [ref=e2680]:
                - text: requestGC
                - link "Direct link to requestGC" [ref=e2681] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#page-request-gc"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: "Added in: v1.48"
              - paragraph [ref=e2682]: Request the page to perform garbage collection. Note that there is no guarantee that all unreachable objects will be collected.
              - paragraph [ref=e2683]:
                - text: This is useful to help detect memory leaks. For example, if your page has a large object
                - code [ref=e2684]: "'suspect'"
                - text: that might be leaked, you can check that it does not leak by using a
                - link "WeakRef" [ref=e2685] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/WeakRef
                  - code [ref=e2686]: WeakRef
                - text: .
              - code [ref=e2690]:
                - generic [ref=e2691]: // 1. In your page, save a WeakRef for the "suspect".
                - generic [ref=e2692]: await page.evaluate(() => globalThis.suspectWeakRef = new WeakRef(suspect));
                - generic [ref=e2693]: // 2. Request garbage collection.
                - generic [ref=e2694]: await page.requestGC();
                - generic [ref=e2695]: // 3. Check that weak ref does not deref to the original object.
                - generic [ref=e2696]: expect(await page.evaluate(() => !globalThis.suspectWeakRef.deref())).toBe(true);
              - paragraph [ref=e2697]:
                - strong [ref=e2698]: Usage
              - code [ref=e2702]:
                - generic [ref=e2703]: await page.requestGC();
              - paragraph [ref=e2704]:
                - strong [ref=e2705]: Returns
              - list [ref=e2706]:
                - listitem [ref=e2707]:
                  - link "Promise" [ref=e2708] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Promise
                  - text: <
                  - link "void" [ref=e2709] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/undefined
                  - text: ">"
                  - link "#" [ref=e2710] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#page-request-gc-return"
              - separator [ref=e2711]
              - heading "requestsDirect link to requests" [level=3] [ref=e2712]:
                - text: requests
                - link "Direct link to requests" [ref=e2713] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#page-requests"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: "Added in: v1.56"
              - paragraph [ref=e2714]:
                - text: Returns up to (currently) 100 last network request from this page. See
                - link "page.on('request')" [ref=e2715] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-event-request
                - text: for more details.
              - paragraph [ref=e2716]: Returned requests should be accessed immediately, otherwise they might be collected to prevent unbounded memory growth as new requests come in. Once collected, retrieving most information about the request is impossible.
              - paragraph [ref=e2717]:
                - text: Note that requests reported through the
                - link "page.on('request')" [ref=e2718] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-event-request
                - text: request are not collected, so there is a trade off between efficient memory usage with
                - link "page.requests()" [ref=e2719] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-requests
                - text: and the amount of available information reported through
                - link "page.on('request')" [ref=e2720] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-event-request
                - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e2721]:
                - strong [ref=e2722]: Usage
              - code [ref=e2726]:
                - generic [ref=e2727]: await page.requests();
              - paragraph [ref=e2728]:
                - strong [ref=e2729]: Returns
              - list [ref=e2730]:
                - listitem [ref=e2731]:
                  - link "Promise" [ref=e2732] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Promise
                  - text: <
                  - link "Array" [ref=e2733] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Array
                  - text: <
                  - link "Request" [ref=e2734] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-request
                  - text: ">>"
                  - link "#" [ref=e2735] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#page-requests-return"
              - separator [ref=e2736]
              - heading "routeDirect link to route" [level=3] [ref=e2737]:
                - text: route
                - link "Direct link to route" [ref=e2738] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#page-route"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: Added before v1.9
              - paragraph [ref=e2739]: Routing provides the capability to modify network requests that are made by a page.
              - paragraph [ref=e2740]: Once routing is enabled, every request matching the url pattern will stall unless it's continued, fulfilled or aborted.
              - generic [ref=e2741]:
                - generic [ref=e2742]:
                  - img [ref=e2744]
                  - text: note
                - paragraph [ref=e2747]: The handler will only be called for the first url if the response is a redirect.
              - generic [ref=e2748]:
                - generic [ref=e2749]:
                  - img [ref=e2751]
                  - text: note
                - paragraph [ref=e2754]:
                  - link "page.route()" [ref=e2755] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-route
                  - text: will not intercept requests intercepted by Service Worker. See
                  - link "this" [ref=e2756] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://github.com/microsoft/playwright/issues/1090
                  - text: issue. We recommend disabling Service Workers when using request interception by setting
                  - link "serviceWorkers" [ref=e2757] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-browser#browser-new-context-option-service-workers
                  - text: to
                  - code [ref=e2758]: "'block'"
                  - text: .
              - generic [ref=e2759]:
                - generic [ref=e2760]:
                  - img [ref=e2762]
                  - text: note
                - paragraph [ref=e2765]:
                  - link "page.route()" [ref=e2766] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-route
                  - text: will not intercept the first request of a popup page. Use
                  - link "browserContext.route()" [ref=e2767] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-route
                  - text: instead.
              - paragraph [ref=e2768]:
                - strong [ref=e2769]: Usage
              - paragraph [ref=e2770]: "An example of a naive handler that aborts all image requests:"
              - code [ref=e2774]:
                - generic [ref=e2775]: const page = await browser.newPage();
                - generic [ref=e2776]: "await page.route('**/*.{png,jpg,jpeg}', route => route.abort());"
                - generic [ref=e2777]: await page.goto('https://example.com');
                - generic [ref=e2778]: await browser.close();
              - paragraph [ref=e2779]: "or the same snippet using a regex pattern instead:"
              - code [ref=e2783]:
                - generic [ref=e2784]: const page = await browser.newPage();
                - generic [ref=e2785]: await page.route(/(\.png$)|(\.jpg$)/, route => route.abort());
                - generic [ref=e2786]: await page.goto('https://example.com');
                - generic [ref=e2787]: await browser.close();
              - paragraph [ref=e2788]: "It is possible to examine the request to decide the route action. For example, mocking all requests that contain some post data, and leaving all other requests as is:"
              - code [ref=e2792]:
                - generic [ref=e2793]: "await page.route('/api/**', async route => {"
                - generic [ref=e2794]: if (route.request().postData().includes('my-string'))
                - generic [ref=e2795]: "await route.fulfill({ body: 'mocked-data' });"
                - generic [ref=e2796]: else
                - generic [ref=e2797]: await route.continue();
                - generic [ref=e2798]: "});"
              - paragraph [ref=e2799]:
                - text: Page routes take precedence over browser context routes (set up with
                - link "browserContext.route()" [ref=e2800] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-route
                - text: ) when request matches both handlers.

              - list [ref=e2878]:
                - listitem [ref=e2879]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e2880]:
                    - code [ref=e2881]: har
                    - link "string" [ref=e2882] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                    - link "#" [ref=e2883] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: "#page-route-from-har-option-har"
                  - paragraph [ref=e2884]:
                    - text: Path to a
                    - link "HAR" [ref=e2885] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: http://www.softwareishard.com/blog/har-12-spec
                    - text: file with prerecorded network data. If
                    - code [ref=e2886]: path
                    - text: is a relative path, then it is resolved relative to the current working directory.
                - listitem [ref=e2887]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e2888]:
                    - code [ref=e2889]: options
                    - link "Object" [ref=e2890] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object
                    - emphasis [ref=e2891]: (optional)
                  - list [ref=e2892]:
                    - listitem [ref=e2893]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2894]:
                        - code [ref=e2895]: notFound
                        - text: "\"abort\" | \"fallback\""
                        - emphasis [ref=e2896]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e2897] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-route-from-har-option-not-found"
                      - list [ref=e2898]:
                        - listitem [ref=e2899]: If set to 'abort' any request not found in the HAR file will be aborted.
                        - listitem [ref=e2900]: If set to 'fallback' missing requests will be sent to the network.
                      - paragraph [ref=e2901]: Defaults to abort.
                    - listitem [ref=e2902]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2903]:
                        - code [ref=e2904]: update
                        - link "boolean" [ref=e2905] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#Boolean_type
                        - emphasis [ref=e2906]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e2907] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-route-from-har-option-update"
                      - paragraph [ref=e2908]:
                        - text: If specified, updates the given HAR with the actual network information instead of serving from file. The file is written to disk when
                        - link "browserContext.close()" [ref=e2909] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-close
                        - text: is called.
                    - listitem [ref=e2910]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2911]:
                        - code [ref=e2912]: updateContent
                        - text: "\"embed\" | \"attach\""
                        - emphasis [ref=e2913]: (optional)
                        - text: "Added in: v1.32"
                        - link "#" [ref=e2914] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-route-from-har-option-update-content"
                      - paragraph [ref=e2915]:
                        - text: Optional setting to control resource content management. If
                        - code [ref=e2916]: attach
                        - text: is specified, resources are persisted as separate files or entries in the ZIP archive. If
                        - code [ref=e2917]: embed
                        - text: is specified, content is stored inline the HAR file.
                    - listitem [ref=e2918]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2919]:
                        - code [ref=e2920]: updateMode
                        - text: "\"full\" | \"minimal\""
                        - emphasis [ref=e2921]: (optional)
                        - text: "Added in: v1.32"
                        - link "#" [ref=e2922] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-route-from-har-option-update-mode"
                      - paragraph [ref=e2923]:
                        - text: When set to
                        - code [ref=e2924]: minimal
                        - text: ", only record information necessary for routing from HAR. This omits sizes, timing, page, cookies, security and other types of HAR information that are not used when replaying from HAR. Defaults to"
                        - code [ref=e2925]: minimal
                        - text: .
                    - listitem [ref=e2926]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e2927]:

                        - link "#" [ref=e2932] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-route-from-har-option-url"
                      - paragraph [ref=e2933]: A glob pattern, regular expression or predicate to match the request URL. Only requests with URL matching the pattern will be served from the HAR file. If not specified, all requests are served from the HAR file.

                      - paragraph [ref=e3017]:
                        - text: When set to
                        - code [ref=e3018]: "\"disabled\""
                        - text: ", stops CSS animations, CSS transitions and Web Animations. Animations get different treatment depending on their duration:"
                      - list [ref=e3019]:
                        - listitem [ref=e3020]:
                          - text: finite animations are fast-forwarded to completion, so they'll fire
                          - code [ref=e3021]: transitionend
                          - text: event.
                        - listitem [ref=e3022]: infinite animations are canceled to initial state, and then played over after the screenshot.
                      - paragraph [ref=e3023]:
                        - text: Defaults to
                        - code [ref=e3024]: "\"allow\""
                        - text: that leaves animations untouched.
                    - listitem [ref=e3025]:

                        - code [ref=e3032]: "\"initial\""

                        - code [ref=e3204]: load

                      - list [ref=e3205]:
                        - listitem [ref=e3206]:
                          - code [ref=e3207]: "'domcontentloaded'"

                          - code [ref=e3208]: DOMContentLoaded
                          - text: event is fired.
                        - listitem [ref=e3209]:
                          - code [ref=e3210]: "'load'"
                          - text: "- consider operation to be finished when the"
                          - code [ref=e3211]: load
                          - text: event is fired.
                        - listitem [ref=e3212]:
                          - code [ref=e3213]: "'networkidle'"
                          - text: "-"
                          - strong [ref=e3214]: DISCOURAGED
                          - text: consider operation to be finished when there are no network connections for at least
                          - code [ref=e3215]: "500"
                          - text: ms. Don't use this method for testing, rely on web assertions to assess readiness instead.
                        - listitem [ref=e3216]:
                          - code [ref=e3217]: "'commit'"
                          - text: "- consider operation to be finished when network response is received and the document started loading."

                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-set-viewport-size
                - text: will resize the page. A lot of websites don't expect phones to change size, so you should set the viewport size before navigating to the page.

                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-set-viewport-size

                  - text: "#"
              - text: Added before v1.9
              - paragraph [ref=e3714]: Returns when the required load state has been reached.
              - paragraph [ref=e3715]:
                - text: This resolves when the page reaches a required load state,
                - code [ref=e3716]: load
                - text: by default. The navigation must have been committed when this method is called. If current document has already reached the required state, resolves immediately.
              - generic [ref=e3717]:
                - generic [ref=e3718]:
                  - img [ref=e3720]

                  - text: Most of the time, this method is not needed because Playwright
                  - link "auto-waits before every action" [ref=e3724] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/actionability
                  - text: .

              - code [ref=e3736]:

                - generic [ref=e3738]: await page.getByRole('button').click(); // Click triggers a popup.
                - generic [ref=e3739]: const popup = await popupPromise;
                - generic [ref=e3740]: await popup.waitForLoadState('domcontentloaded'); // Wait for the 'DOMContentLoaded' event.
                - generic [ref=e3741]: console.log(await popup.title()); // Popup is ready to use.

                    - text: Optional load state to wait for, defaults to
                    - code [ref=e3751]: load
                    - text: ". If the state has been already reached while loading current document, the method resolves immediately. Can be one of:"
                  - list [ref=e3752]:
                    - listitem [ref=e3753]:
                      - code [ref=e3754]: "'load'"
                      - text: "- wait for the"
                      - code [ref=e3755]: load
                      - text: event to be fired.

                      - code [ref=e3757]: "'domcontentloaded'"
                      - text: "- wait for the"

                      - code [ref=e3760]: "'networkidle'"
                      - text: "-"

                      - text: wait until there are no network connections for at least
                      - code [ref=e3762]: "500"
                      - text: ms. Don't use this method for testing, rely on web assertions to assess readiness instead.

                        - code [ref=e3963]: load

                      - list [ref=e3964]:

                          - code [ref=e3966]: "'domcontentloaded'"

                          - code [ref=e3967]: DOMContentLoaded
                          - text: event is fired.

                          - code [ref=e3969]: "'load'"
                          - text: "- consider operation to be finished when the"
                          - code [ref=e3970]: load
                          - text: event is fired.
                        - listitem [ref=e3971]:
                          - code [ref=e3972]: "'networkidle'"
                          - text: "-"
                          - strong [ref=e3973]: DISCOURAGED
                          - text: consider operation to be finished when there are no network connections for at least
                          - code [ref=e3974]: "500"
                          - text: ms. Don't use this method for testing, rely on web assertions to assess readiness instead.
                        - listitem [ref=e3975]:
                          - code [ref=e3976]: "'commit'"
                          - text: "- consider operation to be finished when network response is received and the document started loading."

              - text: Added before v1.9
              - paragraph [ref=e4163]: Emitted when the page crashes. Browser pages might crash if they try to allocate too much memory. When the page crashes, ongoing and subsequent operations will throw.
              - paragraph [ref=e4164]: "The most common way to deal with crashes is to catch an exception:"
              - code [ref=e4168]:
                - generic [ref=e4169]: "try {"
                - generic [ref=e4170]: // Crash might happen during a click.
                - generic [ref=e4171]: await page.click('button');
                - generic [ref=e4172]: // Or while waiting for an event.
                - generic [ref=e4173]: await page.waitForEvent('popup');
                - generic [ref=e4174]: "} catch (e) {"
                - generic [ref=e4175]: // When the page crashes, exception message contains 'crash'.
                - generic [ref=e4176]: "}"
              - paragraph [ref=e4177]:
                - strong [ref=e4178]: Usage

                - generic [ref=e4183]: "page.on('crash', data => {});"

              - paragraph [ref=e4377]:
                - text: Emitted when the page opens a new tab or window. This event is emitted in addition to the
                - link "browserContext.on('page')" [ref=e4378] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-event-page
                - text: ", but only for popups relevant to this page."
              - paragraph [ref=e4379]:
                - text: The earliest moment that page is available is when it has navigated to the initial url. For example, when opening a popup with
                - code [ref=e4380]: window.open('http://example.com')
                - text: ", this event will fire when the network request to \""
                - link "http://example.com" [ref=e4381] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: http://example.com
                - text: "\" is done and its response has started loading in the popup. If you would like to route/listen to this network request, use"
                - link "browserContext.route()" [ref=e4382] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-route
                - text: and
                - link "browserContext.on('request')" [ref=e4383] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-event-request
                - text: respectively instead of similar methods on the
                - link "Page" [ref=e4384] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page
                - text: .

                - generic [ref=e4392]: const popup = await popupPromise;
                - generic [ref=e4393]: console.log(await popup.evaluate('location.href'));

                - listitem [ref=e4780]:
                  - text: Find an element matching
                  - link "selector" [ref=e4781] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-check-option-selector
                  - text: . If there is none, wait until a matching element is attached to the DOM.
                - listitem [ref=e4782]: Ensure that matched element is a checkbox or a radio input. If not, this method throws. If the element is already checked, this method returns immediately.
                - listitem [ref=e4783]:
                  - text: Wait for
                  - link "actionability" [ref=e4784] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/actionability
                  - text: checks on the matched element, unless
                  - link "force" [ref=e4785] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-check-option-force
                  - text: option is set. If the element is detached during the checks, the whole action is retried.
                - listitem [ref=e4786]: Scroll the element into view if needed.
                - listitem [ref=e4787]:
                  - text: Use
                  - link "page.mouse" [ref=e4788] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-mouse
                  - text: to click in the center of the element.
                - listitem [ref=e4789]: Ensure that the element is now checked. If not, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e4790]:
                - text: When all steps combined have not finished during the specified
                - link "timeout" [ref=e4791] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-check-option-timeout
                - text: ", this method throws a"
                - link "TimeoutError" [ref=e4792] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-timeouterror
                - text: . Passing zero timeout disables this.

                - text: Under the hood, it creates an instance of an event based on the given
                - link "type" [ref=e5231] [cursor=pointer]:

                - link "eventInit" [ref=e5232] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-dispatch-event-option-event-init
                - text: properties and dispatches it on the element. Events are
                - code [ref=e5233]: composed
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e5234]: cancelable
                - text: and bubble by default.

                - text: checks, focuses the element, fills it and triggers an
                - code [ref=e5337]: input
                - text: event after filling. Note that you can pass an empty string to clear the input field.
              - paragraph [ref=e5338]:

                - code [ref=e5341]: "[contenteditable]"

                - code [ref=e5342]: <label>

                - link "control" [ref=e5343] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/HTMLLabelElement/control

              - paragraph [ref=e5569]:
                - text: This method hovers over an element matching
                - link "selector" [ref=e5570] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-hover-option-selector
                - text: "by performing the following steps:"
              - list [ref=e5571]:
                - listitem [ref=e5572]:
                  - text: Find an element matching
                  - link "selector" [ref=e5573] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-hover-option-selector
                  - text: . If there is none, wait until a matching element is attached to the DOM.
                - listitem [ref=e5574]:
                  - text: Wait for
                  - link "actionability" [ref=e5575] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/actionability
                  - text: checks on the matched element, unless
                  - link "force" [ref=e5576] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-hover-option-force
                  - text: option is set. If the element is detached during the checks, the whole action is retried.
                - listitem [ref=e5577]: Scroll the element into view if needed.
                - listitem [ref=e5578]:
                  - text: Use
                  - link "page.mouse" [ref=e5579] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-mouse
                  - text: to hover over the center of the element, or the specified
                  - link "position" [ref=e5580] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-hover-option-position
                  - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e5581]:
                - text: When all steps combined have not finished during the specified
                - link "timeout" [ref=e5582] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-hover-option-timeout
                - text: ", this method throws a"
                - link "TimeoutError" [ref=e5583] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-timeouterror
                - text: . Passing zero timeout disables this.

                - text: "-"

                - text: ","

                - text: "-"

                - text: ","

                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e6291]: Backspace
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e6292]: Tab
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e6293]: Delete
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e6294]: Escape
                - text: ","

                - text: ","

                - text: ","

                - text: ","

                - text: ","

                - code [ref=e6301]: PageUp
                - text: ","

                - text: ","

                - text: ", etc."
              - paragraph [ref=e6304]:
                - text: "Following modification shortcuts are also supported:"
                - code [ref=e6305]: Shift
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e6306]: Control
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e6307]: Alt
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e6308]: Meta
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e6309]: ShiftLeft
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e6310]: ControlOrMeta
                - text: .

                - text: resolves to
                - code [ref=e6312]: Control
                - text: on Windows and Linux and to
                - code [ref=e6313]: Meta
                - text: on macOS.
              - paragraph [ref=e6314]:
                - text: Holding down
                - code [ref=e6315]: Shift
                - text: will type the text that corresponds to the
                - link "key" [ref=e6316] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-press-option-key
                - text: in the upper case.
              - paragraph [ref=e6317]:
                - text: If
                - link "key" [ref=e6318] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-press-option-key
                - text: is a single character, it is case-sensitive, so the values
                - code [ref=e6319]: a
                - text: and
                - code [ref=e6320]: A
                - text: will generate different respective texts.
              - paragraph [ref=e6321]:
                - text: Shortcuts such as
                - code [ref=e6322]: "key: \"Control+o\""
                - text: ","
                - code [ref=e6323]: "key: \"Control++"
                - text: or
                - code [ref=e6324]: "key: \"Control+Shift+T\""
                - text: are supported as well. When specified with the modifier, modifier is pressed and being held while the subsequent key is being pressed.

                - text: ", waits for"
                - link "actionability" [ref=e6427] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/actionability
                - text: checks, waits until all specified options are present in the
                - code [ref=e6428]: <select>
                - text: element and selects these options.
              - paragraph [ref=e6429]:
                - text: If the target element is not a
                - code [ref=e6430]: <select>
                - text: element, this method throws an error. However, if the element is inside the
                - code [ref=e6431]: <label>
                - text: element that has an associated
                - link "control" [ref=e6432] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/HTMLLabelElement/control
                - text: ", the control will be used instead."
              - paragraph [ref=e6433]: Returns the array of option values that have been successfully selected.
              - paragraph [ref=e6434]:
                - text: Triggers a
                - code [ref=e6435]: change
                - text: and
                - code [ref=e6436]: input
                - text: event once all the provided options have been selected.
              - paragraph [ref=e6437]:

              - paragraph [ref=e6563]:
                - text: This method checks or unchecks an element matching
                - link "selector" [ref=e6564] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-set-checked-option-selector
                - text: "by performing the following steps:"
              - list [ref=e6565]:
                - listitem [ref=e6566]:
                  - text: Find an element matching
                  - link "selector" [ref=e6567] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-set-checked-option-selector
                  - text: . If there is none, wait until a matching element is attached to the DOM.
                - listitem [ref=e6568]: Ensure that matched element is a checkbox or a radio input. If not, this method throws.
                - listitem [ref=e6569]: If the element already has the right checked state, this method returns immediately.
                - listitem [ref=e6570]:
                  - text: Wait for
                  - link "actionability" [ref=e6571] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/actionability
                  - text: checks on the matched element, unless
                  - link "force" [ref=e6572] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-set-checked-option-force
                  - text: option is set. If the element is detached during the checks, the whole action is retried.
                - listitem [ref=e6573]: Scroll the element into view if needed.
                - listitem [ref=e6574]:
                  - text: Use
                  - link "page.mouse" [ref=e6575] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-mouse
                  - text: to click in the center of the element.
                - listitem [ref=e6576]: Ensure that the element is now checked or unchecked. If not, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e6577]:
                - text: When all steps combined have not finished during the specified
                - link "timeout" [ref=e6578] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-set-checked-option-timeout
                - text: ", this method throws a"
                - link "TimeoutError" [ref=e6579] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-timeouterror
                - text: . Passing zero timeout disables this.
              - paragraph [ref=e6580]:

                - code [ref=e6695]: filePaths

                - code [ref=e6696]: "[webkitdirectory]"
                - text: attribute, only a single directory path is supported.

              - paragraph [ref=e6802]:
                - text: This method taps an element matching
                - link "selector" [ref=e6803] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-tap-option-selector
                - text: "by performing the following steps:"
              - list [ref=e6804]:
                - listitem [ref=e6805]:
                  - text: Find an element matching
                  - link "selector" [ref=e6806] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-tap-option-selector
                  - text: . If there is none, wait until a matching element is attached to the DOM.
                - listitem [ref=e6807]:
                  - text: Wait for
                  - link "actionability" [ref=e6808] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/actionability
                  - text: checks on the matched element, unless
                  - link "force" [ref=e6809] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-tap-option-force
                  - text: option is set. If the element is detached during the checks, the whole action is retried.
                - listitem [ref=e6810]: Scroll the element into view if needed.
                - listitem [ref=e6811]:
                  - text: Use
                  - link "page.touchscreen" [ref=e6812] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-touchscreen
                  - text: to tap the center of the element, or the specified
                  - link "position" [ref=e6813] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-tap-option-position
                  - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e6814]:
                - text: When all steps combined have not finished during the specified
                - link "timeout" [ref=e6815] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-tap-option-timeout
                - text: ", this method throws a"
                - link "TimeoutError" [ref=e6816] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-timeouterror
                - text: . Passing zero timeout disables this.

                  - link "hasTouch" [ref=e6825] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-browser#browser-new-context-option-has-touch
                  - text: option of the browser context is false.
