              - paragraph [ref=e7098]:
                - text: This method unchecks an element matching
                - link "selector" [ref=e7099] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-uncheck-option-selector
                - text: "by performing the following steps:"
              - list [ref=e7100]:
                - listitem [ref=e7101]:
                  - text: Find an element matching
                  - link "selector" [ref=e7102] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-uncheck-option-selector
                  - text: . If there is none, wait until a matching element is attached to the DOM.
                - listitem [ref=e7103]: Ensure that matched element is a checkbox or a radio input. If not, this method throws. If the element is already unchecked, this method returns immediately.
                - listitem [ref=e7104]:
                  - text: Wait for
                  - link "actionability" [ref=e7105] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/actionability
                  - text: checks on the matched element, unless
                  - link "force" [ref=e7106] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-uncheck-option-force
                  - text: option is set. If the element is detached during the checks, the whole action is retried.
                - listitem [ref=e7107]: Scroll the element into view if needed.
                - listitem [ref=e7108]:
                  - text: Use
                  - link "page.mouse" [ref=e7109] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-mouse
                  - text: to click in the center of the element.
                - listitem [ref=e7110]: Ensure that the element is now unchecked. If not, this method throws.
              - paragraph [ref=e7111]:
                - text: When all steps combined have not finished during the specified
                - link "timeout" [ref=e7112] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-uncheck-option-timeout
                - text: ", this method throws a"
                - link "TimeoutError" [ref=e7113] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-timeouterror
                - text: . Passing zero timeout disables this.
              - paragraph [ref=e7114]:

              - paragraph [ref=e7221]:
                - text: Waits for the main frame navigation and returns the main resource response. In case of multiple redirects, the navigation will resolve with the response of the last redirect. In case of navigation to a different anchor or navigation due to History API usage, the navigation will resolve with
                - code [ref=e7222]: "null"
                - text: .
              - paragraph [ref=e7223]:
                - strong [ref=e7224]: Usage
              - paragraph [ref=e7225]:
                - text: This resolves when the page navigates to a new URL or reloads. It is useful for when you run code which will indirectly cause the page to navigate. e.g. The click target has an
                - code [ref=e7226]: onclick
                - text: handler that triggers navigation from a
                - code [ref=e7227]: setTimeout
                - text: ". Consider this example:"

                    - listitem [ref=e7277]:

                        - text: When to consider operation succeeded, defaults to
                        - code [ref=e7283]: load
                        - text: ". Events can be either:"
                      - list [ref=e7284]:

                          - code [ref=e7286]: "'domcontentloaded'"
                          - text: "- consider operation to be finished when the"
                          - code [ref=e7287]: DOMContentLoaded
                          - text: event is fired.
                        - listitem [ref=e7288]:
                          - code [ref=e7289]: "'load'"
                          - text: "- consider operation to be finished when the"
                          - code [ref=e7290]: load
                          - text: event is fired.
                        - listitem [ref=e7291]:
                          - code [ref=e7292]: "'networkidle'"
                          - text: "-"
                          - strong [ref=e7293]: DISCOURAGED
                          - text: consider operation to be finished when there are no network connections for at least
                          - code [ref=e7294]: "500"
                          - text: ms. Don't use this method for testing, rely on web assertions to assess readiness instead.
                        - listitem [ref=e7295]:
                          - code [ref=e7296]: "'commit'"
                          - text: "- consider operation to be finished when network response is received and the document started loading."

              - paragraph [ref=e7317]:
                - text: Returns when element specified by selector satisfies
                - link "state" [ref=e7318] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-wait-for-selector-option-state
                - text: option. Returns
                - code [ref=e7319]: "null"
                - text: if waiting for
                - code [ref=e7320]: hidden
                - text: or
                - code [ref=e7321]: detached
                - text: .
              - generic [ref=e7322]:
                - generic [ref=e7323]:
                  - img [ref=e7325]
                  - text: note
                - paragraph [ref=e7328]:
                  - text: Playwright automatically waits for element to be ready before performing an action. Using
                  - link "Locator" [ref=e7329] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator
                  - text: objects and web-first assertions makes the code wait-for-selector-free.
              - paragraph [ref=e7330]:
                - text: Wait for the
                - link "selector" [ref=e7331] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-wait-for-selector-option-selector
                - text: to satisfy
                - link "state" [ref=e7332] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-wait-for-selector-option-state
                - text: option (either appear/disappear from dom, or become visible/hidden). If at the moment of calling the method
                - link "selector" [ref=e7333] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-wait-for-selector-option-selector
                - text: already satisfies the condition, the method will return immediately. If the selector doesn't satisfy the condition for the
                - link "timeout" [ref=e7334] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-wait-for-selector-option-timeout
                - text: milliseconds, the function will throw.
              - paragraph [ref=e7335]:
                - strong [ref=e7336]: Usage
              - paragraph [ref=e7337]: "This method works across navigations:"
              - code [ref=e7341]:
                - generic [ref=e7342]: "const { chromium } = require('playwright'); // Or 'firefox' or 'webkit'."
                - generic [ref=e7343]: "(async () => {"
                - generic [ref=e7344]: const browser = await chromium.launch();
                - generic [ref=e7345]: const page = await browser.newPage();
                - generic [ref=e7346]: "for (const currentURL of ['https://google.com', 'https://bbc.com']) {"
                - generic [ref=e7347]: await page.goto(currentURL);
                - generic [ref=e7348]: const element = await page.waitForSelector('img');
                - generic [ref=e7349]: "console.log('Loaded image: ' + await element.getAttribute('src'));"
                - generic [ref=e7350]: "}"
                - generic [ref=e7351]: await browser.close();
                - generic [ref=e7352]: "})();"
              - paragraph [ref=e7353]:
                - strong [ref=e7354]: Arguments
              - list [ref=e7355]:
                - listitem [ref=e7356]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e7357]:
                    - code [ref=e7358]: selector
                    - link "string" [ref=e7359] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#String_type
                    - link "#" [ref=e7360] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: "#page-wait-for-selector-option-selector"
                  - paragraph [ref=e7361]: A selector to query for.
                - listitem [ref=e7362]:
                  - paragraph [ref=e7363]:
                    - code [ref=e7364]: options
                    - link "Object" [ref=e7365] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object
                    - emphasis [ref=e7366]: (optional)
                  - list [ref=e7367]:
                    - listitem [ref=e7368]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e7369]:
                        - code [ref=e7370]: state
                        - text: "\"attached\" | \"detached\" | \"visible\" | \"hidden\""
                        - emphasis [ref=e7371]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e7372] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-wait-for-selector-option-state"
                      - paragraph [ref=e7373]:
                        - text: Defaults to
                        - code [ref=e7374]: "'visible'"
                        - text: ". Can be either:"
                      - list [ref=e7375]:
                        - listitem [ref=e7376]:
                          - code [ref=e7377]: "'attached'"
                          - text: "- wait for element to be present in DOM."
                        - listitem [ref=e7378]:
                          - code [ref=e7379]: "'detached'"
                          - text: "- wait for element to not be present in DOM."
                        - listitem [ref=e7380]:
                          - code [ref=e7381]: "'visible'"
                          - text: "- wait for element to have non-empty bounding box and no"
                          - code [ref=e7382]: visibility:hidden
                          - text: . Note that element without any content or with
                          - code [ref=e7383]: display:none
                          - text: has an empty bounding box and is not considered visible.
                        - listitem [ref=e7384]:
                          - code [ref=e7385]: "'hidden'"
                          - text: "- wait for element to be either detached from DOM, or have an empty bounding box or"
                          - code [ref=e7386]: visibility:hidden
                          - text: . This is opposite to the
                          - code [ref=e7387]: "'visible'"
                          - text: option.
                    - listitem [ref=e7388]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e7389]:
                        - code [ref=e7390]: strict
                        - link "boolean" [ref=e7391] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#Boolean_type
                        - emphasis [ref=e7392]: (optional)
                        - text: "Added in: v1.14"
                        - link "#" [ref=e7393] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-wait-for-selector-option-strict"
                      - paragraph [ref=e7394]: When true, the call requires selector to resolve to a single element. If given selector resolves to more than one element, the call throws an exception.
                    - listitem [ref=e7395]:
                      - paragraph [ref=e7396]:
                        - code [ref=e7397]: timeout
                        - link "number" [ref=e7398] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Data_structures#Number_type
                        - emphasis [ref=e7399]: (optional)
                        - link "#" [ref=e7400] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: "#page-wait-for-selector-option-timeout"
                      - paragraph [ref=e7401]:
                        - text: Maximum time in milliseconds. Defaults to
                        - code [ref=e7402]: "0"
                        - text: "- no timeout. The default value can be changed via"
                        - code [ref=e7403]: actionTimeout
                        - text: option in the config, or by using the
                        - link "browserContext.setDefaultTimeout()" [ref=e7404] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-browsercontext#browser-context-set-default-timeout
                        - text: or
                        - link "page.setDefaultTimeout()" [ref=e7405] [cursor=pointer]:
                          - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-set-default-timeout
                        - text: methods.
              - paragraph [ref=e7406]:
                - strong [ref=e7407]: Returns
              - list [ref=e7408]:
                - listitem [ref=e7409]:
                  - link "Promise" [ref=e7410] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Promise
                  - text: <
                  - link "null" [ref=e7411] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/null
                  - text: "|"
                  - link "ElementHandle" [ref=e7412] [cursor=pointer]:

                  - text: ">"
                  - link "#" [ref=e7413] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: "#page-wait-for-selector-return"
              - separator [ref=e7414]
              - heading "waitForTimeoutDirect link to waitForTimeout" [level=3] [ref=e7415]:
                - text: waitForTimeout
                - link "Direct link to waitForTimeout" [ref=e7416] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: "#page-wait-for-timeout"
                  - text: "#"
              - text: Added before v1.9
              - generic [ref=e7417]:
                - generic [ref=e7418]:
                  - img [ref=e7420]
                  - text: Discouraged
                - paragraph [ref=e7423]:
                  - text: Never wait for timeout in production. Tests that wait for time are inherently flaky. Use
                  - link "Locator" [ref=e7424] [cursor=pointer]:
                    - /url: /docs/api/class-locator
                  - text: actions and web assertions that wait automatically.
              - paragraph [ref=e7425]:
                - text: Waits for the given
                - link "timeout" [ref=e7426] [cursor=pointer]:
                  - /url: /docs/api/class-page#page-wait-for-timeout-option-timeout
                - text: in milliseconds.
              - paragraph [ref=e7427]:
                - text: Note that
                - code [ref=e7428]: page.waitForTimeout()
                - text: should only be used for debugging. Tests using the timer in production are going to be flaky. Use signals such as network events, selectors becoming visible and others instead.
              - paragraph [ref=e7429]:
                - strong [ref=e7430]: Usage
              - code [ref=e7434]:
                - generic [ref=e7435]: // wait for 1 second
                - generic [ref=e7436]: await page.waitForTimeout(1000);
              - paragraph [ref=e7437]:
                - strong [ref=e7438]: Arguments

                    - link "#" [ref=e7444] [cursor=pointer]:
                      - /url: "#page-wait-for-timeout-option-timeout"
                  - paragraph [ref=e7445]: A timeout to wait for
